Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Therefore, he can hardly work, and nevertheless it seems to me that it is better to leave him alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	of cauterization of the pleura
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The ancients said that one should perform cauterizations on the pleura with roots of aristolochia, and in this manner:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	take a root of aristolochia as long as you can find, the largest possible, and let it be dry, and let it be as thick and as long as your two fingers;
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and grind it into oil, and dip it in fire, and perform the cauterization between the shoulder and the neck, and perform two small cauterizations a little lower on the part that is below the beard;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	And apply cauterization between the fifth rib and the sixth, declining a little backwards;
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	and apply one cauterization in the chest, and another on the stomach, and one between the shoulders, and two on the sides of the chest opposite the cauterization which is between the shoulders;
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press with your hand, but make it open as in applying an ointment.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And the authorities said that no man should use fire cauterization on a similar rash, and they warm it and put it between the ribs, until it comes to that abscess;
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and this is without pain, as we have said concerning the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear that the patient will die now, or a fistula comes which cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the bladder
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the tooth that we have spoken of in the divisions of treatments, and it does not profit, then there are three manners of cautery that are good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	One of the manners is that you make three or four cauteries, in a row according to the length of the tooth, according to the shape of the cautery of the flesh that we have spoken of before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand on the entire cautery, and let the patient sit up on his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another manner of cautery is that you heat the cautery that has two nerves, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the skin that is near the tooth, or where the cold of the patient comes from the left side, and let the elevation that you lift the skin according to the skin, according to the length of the body, and the cautery be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After that burn the inflamed areas until the heart is perceived from the other side, and then apply the cauterization, and thus in this way there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you want, then cauterize all of the cauterization to three areas.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the cure when it has obtained purification by long tension, and this is better than the other cures mentioned before.
de ydropisie	of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not suitable for droptics, except in the manner that is called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure according to the methods that we have spoken of in divisions, and your cure does not profit me, then it is necessary that you do four cauterizations around the navel, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one on the right side.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterization be carefully applied near the spinal cord.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cauterization open for a long and tense purging, and do not neglect the treatment of the disease after the cauterization;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing will hasten, and the two intentions will come together with the aid of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cauterization for the belly should be a spike which we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what has been set forth here before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who has dropsy, and are full of watery cysts, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the thumb and the little finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cauterization without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much by depth, thus would be the outer layer of the citrine, and let the cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After that, apply on both legs two cauteries, one on each leg at the point of the cullet or knee;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauteries be on the long, one below the kneecap in front and the other behind, in the middle of the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauteries on for a long time without removing them, until the wound has issued;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the treatment of the other treatments that we have spoken of.
de la menoison	of the mentions
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a discharge from the belly comes from cold and moisture, so that the retaining and digestive virtues which are in the stomach and intestines are weakened, and cannot be cured by methods of treatments;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and of strong virtue, then apply a large cauterization on the stomach according to what has been spoken of before, or the stomach cauterization, to cauterize in a circle;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and 4 cauteries around the subtle navel for every subtle cauterization of the spine, and 2 cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, have it cauterized on the thumb, and one cauterization on each heel, and two small cauterizations on the stomach below the navel, for the treatment is beneficial when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are at the foundation, or one or several, and are old and are of thick cold and moist humors corrupted, and are treated as we have said in sections, and it does not benefit, then make cauterizations:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	3 on the spine of the back, which is all divided into small portions and a little triangle, and 1 cauterization below the navel, 2 fingers.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is chilled, and the food does not digest, and one sees the face swollen, then one applies the large cautery on the stomach, as it was previously stated, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with all the clamp cauteries;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery be applied for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing, leave it so that it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the fleshiness which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut into thelul, heat the cautery which seems to relieve, and then apply it all burned on the cut thelul;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and leave it so that your hand reaches the birth of the vein, where the blood flows without being cut;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this one or two times, and if there is much of thelul, then cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	After the treatment of profitable members as long as they are healthy;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cauter on the ulcer, it will have more aid.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound badly healed
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear cutting or surgical treatment, which we will discuss in its place, then comes a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there comes a fistula, and it is inflamed and irritated by putrid matter and rotten humors, then the doctor will prove with a subtle thread, and be careful that you know the depth of the thread as much as it has.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cauter that seems to be in order, and put it in the fistula according to the quantity that the thread has entered, and renew the cauter as long as those rotten and corrupt bodies are burned, one time, or two, or three, according to the quantity of what is needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of the nerves that are beneath, and of the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and to the intestine, beware of these places, and do not make those wounds that are in the flesh, and think that it is not a perforating.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after the cure, the flesh as long as it is healthy, and if the wound is healed, and the materials are pushed back together at length, then know that the wound is entirely healthy;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the materials are not pushed back, know that the flesh is torn, and the bone is corrupted at the source;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus like one of those things that we will tell about in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain of cold comes to the kidneys, and of great swelling, and it does not take the shape of a woman, then it is necessary that you perform cauterization on the kidneys on one side and on the other with the clavicle cautery that we have spoken of before;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we have the cauterizations in a straight line, there will be three cauteries, and they will provide greater aid.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and fragile from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then make a cauterization on the outer part above the bladder, where the hairs of the pubic area begin, and to the right and to the left, and let each cauterization be as long as the width of a thumb;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make a cauterization on the back, or two if you are in need of it;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the cauterizations be arranged according to the previously described form.
de la marris	of the liver
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the liver is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception because of this, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends are delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, they feel great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is suitable to make three cauterizations around the navel, as we have said concerning the cauterization of the bladder, and two cauterizations on the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauterizations be done with a key, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous humors descend to the box of the thigh, and for this reason it moves from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when one measures them together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and the place of separation is found, then it is suitable that you cauterize the patient on the box of the thigh with a cauterization similar to a circle, and mark before the place around the box as it turns, so that the box is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if there are cauteries such as those with which one cauterizes the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauteries are not present, then make three cauteries of the large olive tree, and let the cauteries be as deep as all the abscesses;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal them until they are healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the thigh
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the thigh, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured of what we have said in the section and the cure is not effective, and the illness is ancient:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then it is necessary that you purge the patient of the thick humors with foul-smelling pills, or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After you make a cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of the cautery is in two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	It is to know assemblage of burning medicines, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cauterization is done in many ways, of which one is the following:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the box of the thigh three triangular cauterizations in this form, and it makes a deep and large wound, and there is between each cauterization a space the size of an egg, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	sometimes one makes a cauterization in the middle on the head of the thigh, because there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see that one cauterizes with a circular cauterization which we have previously spoken of in the dislocation of the thigh;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it in such a way that the circle encompasses the entire thigh, and all the spaces around the heart are dry.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the manner in which it is done for sciatica, when the pain is in the thigh, and does not seem to reach either the hip or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it reaches the hip and the leg, have two cauteries made there where the patient says the pain is, and one cauterization above the knee four fingers, on the left side a little;
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cautery be applied with a warm cloth, and let the thickness of the cauterization be that of a leather strap;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two fingers from the foot or near the ankle, then cauterize there where he feels the pain three points or four at the cauterization which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it is necessary, have more made;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if he knows that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, have a cauterization made with the cloth cauterization or circular one, and take great care in all your cauteries that you do not leave the cauterization so long that you burn the nerves and the large arteries, and that you do not cause the patient more nuisance and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who had cauterization on the leg near the foot, and it let them so that the leg became entirely swollen, and the foot also, and it was pierced and corrupted to the foot.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a abdominal solution where he got death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two places together, perform cauterization in one and in the other, in this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men said regarding the cauterization of the thigh, that this is the method: make an iron instrument and let it be as thick as a walnut, or a little less, and let it be hollow and let one hollow be joined to another with the space of a nut.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the hollows be open on two sides, and also be like nuts, and have an iron hand well made;
et c’est li forme:	and it is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is entirely red and gives off a sweet scent, and then apply it to the box of the patient's ankle, and turn on the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and let the cautery be applied once the fire cautery is ready and let it be for three hours;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make a plaster of butter, and let the wound be covered for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of the joint until it is healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we should use little of this cautery because of its danger, and few see those who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and however these are good cauteries, which one can suffer, and where they adhere to.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The medical burning cauteries are that you make an instrument with notches in which descends the margin of the door, and let it be of copper or iron with a long edge, and in height two nuts, and between each one the quantity of the thickness of a die;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and let them be open downwards and upwards, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Afterwards put on the bandage of the thigh to the patient lying on their healthy side, and press your hand much on the bandage of the thigh;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	afterwards put it between the two circles of the warm water which is warmed by the fire a little, and let it be for an hour or ten, and let the patient suffer from the heat and the burning of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it finds mortification as from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the mortifications have passed, raise your hand with the instrument and lift the thigh of warm water, and let it be for three hours, and put on a poultice as long as what is black from the eschar remains;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it be for three hours that the purulence stays in the strait;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the last aid after the treatment of wounds as long as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended to the thigh or to the leg, make an instrument that holds according to what you have done on the injured limb;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the manner of warm water, and I have written it or treated about the rectification of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkaline substance and living lime, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or it should have a small hole through which the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put that pot in another well-plugged pot, and put on it the alkaline substance and lime and sweet water, as much as there is of the powder when you have well sprinkled it with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it be so until it descends to the water and freezes or congeals, then take all that water, and throw it on hot coals and on quicklime as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very sharp and will be administered in many medical treatments and in cauterizations of other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it makes work like fire, and also other medicines that one cauterizes well the haunch thus as thesis and myrrh and lime with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure in which a man was cured of the pain of the haunch and of the sciatic vein, and praised it highly, and said that no other cure was needed, and that he was healthy at once when this cure was made, and he bathed as he teaches hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And apply in a similar way that you press the green fresh and dry litargire, and bruise it much with a bit of grease, and put it on the thigh and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is, and the injury;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and let it be for three hours and according to the quantity that the patient does not feel the burning anymore.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter into a bath so that his body is warmed a little, and make him enter into bed, and the pain will go away completely and he will be healthy.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that one should not use cauterization of such medicines unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with threads of linen, it helps much;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cauterization should be done in a similar way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the knee and the fat of old oil, and put it on the pit that is between the thumb of the foot and the other called the heel pit.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry fibers of goat's kidney, and dipping them in fire until they are charcoal, and then putting them on the wool, and leaving them there until they are stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do it again thus, and do not stop doing it until you think by sensation that it comes to the bone, and that the pain is eased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this kind of cauterization is called "cauterization of the goat".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, either from a blow or from percussion or from too great evacuation, or from similar things of cold matter spread, none of these things is worth cauterization, except for that which comes from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after this that the patient is treated with foul-smelling pills or other similar things, that they are applied to the back, where the pain is, three signed lines of inch, and in each line a cautery or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can suffer;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and let the cauteries be made according to the cautery that is called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see fit, make three or four cauteries at the middle clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Many times this sickness comes to little children, and the signs of the onset are that they have a constricted arm when they get up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you will find in the upper part of the spine of the back and in the appearance that comes on the other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you judge it to be cured, then cauterize it with the cautery of the vertebra according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cautery touches each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, that the cautery around the spine pricks two or three lines, and the points are close to one another.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the cure, anoint the limb as long as it is healthy according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply cautery in awkwardness which is near a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the pain of the joints is from moistures that are spread to each member of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which the doctors call "podagra" properly, and when it is of a cold cause and cures of medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauteries in such manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make many cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary that you prick on the face of the foot, then make a cautery at the entire area where one calls «point».
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come near the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, then make a cautery on each knee three or four cauteries of each part, to all the olive-tree-like cautery.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you have more of a trade, if you make more, but do not hold your hand further than the length that the shinbone is long.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend near the knee and to the back, then administer the cautery that we have spoken of in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then make pricks around the forearm two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if a point of pain remains in the fingers, then make pricks on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come near the joints or near the shoulders, cauterize each part, and give good governance to the patient and apply remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make him have good governance and you purge phlegm, he will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the spleen or liver (or possibly 'spleen' alone
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture comes into the anguish, and the intestines fall to the groin and it is newly, then it is necessary that when you cure the wound, that you do not touch the one that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things that loosen the belly, so that the feces come down from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after making him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his arm as long as the intestine is being repaired, and apply them to your hands, and sign from below the rupture on the bone of the hip, and make a sign that is similar to half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the cautery of what kind it is:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it becomes white and throws away its sensibilities.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the bowels to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and let the minister guide your hand so that they do not turn back;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and open well the thighs of the patient, and put one cushion and one servant on the thighs, and another on the back who holds the hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then put the cautery on the sign with all your hand, and hold it straight and hold it as long as you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, then recommend it again another time until you come to the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and guard subtly that the bowel does not protrude when you perform the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that by this the patients do not die, or other evils.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not come near to the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to the measure of their bones, and for large people also large according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days cure the limb from the cautery of tar until the eschar is removed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after curing other ulcers until it be healed, and let the patient lie on his back for forty days until the wound is well dried;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that their bandages be tightened for a long time, so that the boils do not burst when he gets up to go to chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wants to get up, a well-made splint should be applied to him, and the poultice for forty other days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let it have good rest, so that it works little and guards against too great a repletion of drinking and eating, and of too high a temperature;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when it makes this teaching then it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will speak later about the treatment of cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures come in other bellies and are connected, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then have made the cautery of the cautery repeated according to its quantity, and let it be the third of the heart;
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients have said that one should be cauterized with a cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the limit of the flesh and make a line across the width above the rupture, and another below, and hold in hand the entire cautery instrument.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and more moderate.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of pain residing in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any member, from a fall or from a blow, and that pain holds for a long time, and the cure of medicine is not effective, then it is necessary that it be cauterized with the cautery that is called "poins", and let the cauteries be according to the length of the member and its smallness and weakness and its virtue and location of torsions and of its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if it is healed from the first cautery, that's good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	if it is not healed by that name, recommend another cautery on top of the first, for such is the custom that it must be changed on the member that is closest to it, for which reason it is necessary that you do the cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	Of mixture
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The mixtures are helped many times by cauterization with great assistance, and likewise the illness that comes from the corruption of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you want to cauterize, beware that the illness is at its beginning, and if it is curable according to what we have said in the division, and does not descend nor stay, and you doubt that the corruption does not infect the whole disease, then make a cauterization on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	Put one cautery on the head to the nue, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two on the two horns, and one behind on the shoulder blade;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and let it be so that the cautery reaches to the bone, and so that the crusts come out from there so that the vapors of the thick humors can come out;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and the cauterization on the mouse according to what it is in front of.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the mixture is spread all over;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is manifestly necessary that you apply the cauterization of these cauterizations that we have mentioned on the head, and one cauterization on the nape of the neck, and two cauterizations on the spine of the neck, and six cauterizations on the spine of the back, and one large one on the pubic area and another below, and two on the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the hips, and two on the tendons of the feet, and one on each joint of the hands and of the feet, and on the palms of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are on the rear calf, that you not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes make a cauterization on the bone of the finger, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more I do of cauterization, the more I do to help, and it brings him profit;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient does not feel a point of pain from the cauterization as much as they feel it, because the body is already entirely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in the manners of the cases.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the cure, treat the limb with flour of wheaten bread and honey and other treatments until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When inflammation comes to any limb and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then have cauterizations on the limb according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization be a little within the thickness of the skin;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the joints until they are healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes a cautery is applied to the hand and to the foot and to the back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus if it is the bone that is swollen;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and in no way should one interfere unless they are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	of Albucasis
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" has grown, and the instruments of medicine are of no value, then cauterize with a cautery somewhat deep, according to the quantity of the thickness of the skin, until the whiteness is removed, and its color is changed;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then treat with flour of vetches and of lentils with rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood of colt and blood of almond, each a part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be wrapped together, and be tied with a bandage, and be elevated to the level as long as it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of cancer by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer comes at the beginning, and you want to stop it, then cauterize with a cauterizing iron which seems a circle, all around the tumor of the cancer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all the wise men said that one should make a cauterization in the middle of the cancer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and however this does not seem good to me, for I fear that it would be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen it happen many times;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and a more proper thing is that it be cauterized around, with the cauterizing iron which is called "circle", as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot be measured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When some people have a disease called "adubelati", and it comes from the excess movement or because of the superfluous humor that it causes, or because of the weakness of the patient when he is decrepit (that is to say too old) and he has little blood, or because of the tension;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you hasten the stopping of moving:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then you cauterize around many small cauteries by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	after that, leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it hastens the stopping of moving.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you perceive the need to cauterize everything, heat the cauterizing iron according to what its form is:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the middle of that disease which is called "adubelati" until the cauterizing iron has penetrated the heart, and let the cauterizing be such that the patient feels relief in some manner so that the course of the corruption is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment as long as he is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment with fire by means of iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of illness is what is called "corrosive", and it is nothing other than a gangrene of a limb, because it eats away the limbs just as fire does dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this illness in a person who can suffer cauterization with fire, then heat the cauterizers little and large, according to what is needed for the person or where the illness is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After the cauterization of all parts, as long as you eradicate all the corruption, and nothing of it remains, that everything which is corrupted should be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let it be for three days, and apply to the limbs cauterized a soothing balm with oil, until the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of painful hemorrhoids there is bleeding.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see that after three days healthy stool does not appear, it's a sign;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then restart the cauterization on that which has remained from the corrupted limbs.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this disease has sometimes been cured with sharp medicine instead of fire cauterization;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nonetheless fire cauterization is of greater aid, and I have already spoken about the treatment with sharp medicine in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take the quantity that you have in your profession.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the pores that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that to the feet through wounds is born a disease which is called "fistula" according to our intention, and is a gross faulty thing that afflicts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization of this disease is according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to know the cautery of fire, and the cautery of hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Cautery of fire is that you heat the cautery head as if it were a feather pen, and made of good iron to the measure that it can pierce the nail from all sides, and that it has subtle edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	afterward put all hot on the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it comes to the bottom of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it stay thus three hours until it induces a purulent discharge;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a plaster of wild mallows bruised with vinegar, and let the plaster stay on all night, and the nail will fall out and will be disrooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the leg of the joint with a warm poultice as long as it is sore.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are turned by various aches in the body, and often occur in the hands and feet, then you must apply cautery of hot water;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in a similar manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a chain of iron or a needle, or a thorn from a vine, and put it on the nail and the flesh, that is to remove the warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and put the chain on so that it penetrates all around, then you put a little warm water, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand in turning so that the edge of the chain comes to the root of the nail, and then find the hot water penetrating just to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer a little the burning of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then let it be, and it will tear out all its roots entirely.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Do this afterward, as long as you scratch all those that are on the body, then cure the ointments which cause the flesh to swell.
li cure dou trembler	the cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some people shiver from cold or from nerves, or from quartan fever or other, it is fitting that you do four cauterizations or four on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cauterization at the foot, and one on the stomach for an olive cauterization;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	it will leave off the shivering, and it will hasten the health from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes appear on the bodies of the sick, boils or pus-filled pustules, which come from corrupted thick materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	If it happens first that they appear to make a cautery on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cautery of the paste of myrtle, from which the point is taken to be seized by fire, or of the root of aristolochia long, or of the lentick cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes the cautery is done at the beginning when it appears, in this manner, and they cannot grow again beforehand, but are broken up the superfluities from which they come, and are healthy;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great outflows of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the surface, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the cautery of the limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very grievous thing to dislocate.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And however when it happens to anyone, if you hasten to put your second finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it very firmly until the blood is stilled beneath your finger, and so that no more comes out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then apply to the fire the olive cauteries, many small and large ones as long as they are well reddened;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take I, either large or small according to the wound and the limb in which the artery is torn, and put the cautery on that vein where you hold with your finger, and hold the cautery as long as the blood is restrained.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it should flow again when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cautery is insufficient, then quickly take another of the cauteries that are by the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing one thing after another until the blood is stanched;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not injure the nerve that is nearby, and that another evil does not come upon the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and be aware that when blood flows from the artery, one cannot very well stop it, especially when the artery is large, unless it is by one of the four methods that we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by a strong tightening of a thread, or by medicines applied which have the power to stanch blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and should be bound and tightened firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	For one will not profit from the binding of tight ligation of cloths or placing hot things on, or other similar things, if it does not help a little.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if it happens to someone and he does not have a doctor or medicine present, then he should put his own index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and press firmly until it is stopped above the wound and above the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move the finger, but rather keep it moist with cold water often so that it is very cold until the blood is congealed and thickened and stopped;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries beforehand about what he needs for cauterizations and for medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This book contains the treatments of stone disease
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have said in the first chapter about every disease for which it is necessary to use fire cauterization, or burning medicine, and the organs and the causes and the symptoms and the forms of the cauterizations;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed that chapter from the head to the feet, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same method because it is easier to find what one looks for.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And thus I entrust to you, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the previous ones about cauteries, and for this reason it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there are often evacuations of blood when opening a vein, and incisions on abscesses, and treatments of wounds, and extractions of arrowheads, and cuttings into stone, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many deaths occur.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you that you do not undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come to be cured.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if there come those who are so accustomed to their illness that they die lightly because of the force of their disease, and the greatness of their evil.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and of these one should have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And of these it is given to whom its meaning is told:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am a leper";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is contemptible.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not necessary that you consent to those who come to you with this condition, but put more caution in your honor than in your desire, and do not open foolishly but wisely that which you are certain of, and that which you can have taken and received.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and make use of prognosis and indication in the treatment of your patients to whom health may be restored;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you to acquire a good reputation, and glory, and a lasting memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dearest son, may our Lord grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration from His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have ordained this chapter by dividing it into sections, according to what it is before the chapter on cauterizations, which I have divided for you from head to feet, because you will find it easier to find what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	of the head full of anguish
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	It is known that this illness comes very often to infants at birth, and when the womb holds too tightly the head of the infant;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it happens for a hidden reason that one is not aware of.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this illness except in infants, and most of those that I have seen hasten death;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason it seems to me that it is better for me to leave the work in some treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw an infant whose head was full of anguish, and the head became so swollen each day that it could not be supported;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and let the moisture flow out as it was dying, and this moisture is gathered from under the bone on the spleen, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the works are such that if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscesses are small, then you make in the head a wide incision;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and let it be as long as two nuts, until the moisture runs;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see to it the form of a spatula or spoon;
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more thick and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the manner of a cross, according to this form;
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is under the bone, and the signs that you see the sutures of the head open on each side, and the water flows out when you press it with your hand inside, and this does not seem to be an answer;
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	if it happens that you make three incisions on the head in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract the moisture entirely from it.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After that, bind the wounds with bandages and powders, and put on wine and oil, and leave it so until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then undo it, and treat the wound with dressings and with ointments, and let the head be strained, and give to eat to the patient dry food without much moisture until the limb is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is that you examine the size of the abscess and the gathering of the pus;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut then the place where the abscess opens, and the filling of the needle, and do it according to what you have the power to do;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and beware that you do not cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and let flow a little blood, so that the patient does not die from lack of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of rheum
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When there is a certain disease called "catarrh" in the eyes or in the chest, and the disease is chronic, and the treatment with medicine is of no benefit, then the last resort is cauterization with what one cuts the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is necessary then, when you cut the veins, that the patient makes his head fall back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after he rubs the place with a coarse cloth until the arteries appear, then the patient tightens his neck against the whole cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein beats, and the limbs of one and the other are after the ears, and a little are raised;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the limbs from the middle, then cut one and the other with a sharp spatula on both sides, as long as the vein extends to the bone, and that is done by the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, push the spatula below the artery and cut upwards, cutting also as the two veins across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, then the blood jumps out continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not appear on feeling, then it is necessary that you measure the quantity of the thickness of three fingers, then mark from the middle and make it go to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and what is necessary to put blood out if it is one sixth, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can suffer, and the replenishment of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the pointed bone of the hip, if the disease that causes abscesses does not come, then strain the wound and bind it, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When ancient migraine comes, and sharp catarrh, because of the moistures of tears and the heats in the temples and old forsakenness and similar things, and it is treated with various methods of cures of medicine and all that does not profit it, then we cauterize the arteries of the temples and their cauterization, as we have related.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of their extraction is that the patient should shave the hairs from his temples, and attend to the artery which opens in the temple, for it opens well by its beating, and is poorly replaced in some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is put back, then remove the patient's neck from certain bandages, then rub the limb with a coarse cloth, and wrap the limb in a warm, damp dressing until the artery appears clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula of which is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scratch the skin lightly until you come to the artery, then draw it up with the pincers, and separate it well from the tendons that are attached to each part;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is delicate, then turn it at the point of the needle, then cut it from that part according to the quantity of the two blood vessels.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, then the blood does not flow at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And let the blood flow from the six hundred, up to three;
